There are quite a few versions of Business International played around the world\r\n\r\nBusiness International is a real-estate board game played between two or six players.\r\n\r\nNow you as a player can create your Monopoly in the world of International Business! The ultimate magnate!\r\n\r\nThe main objective of the game is to force our opponents into bankruptcy by trading i.e. buying, selling and developing different pieces of property.\r\n\r\nThe game board consists of 40 different spaces containing twenty-eight properties: [twenty-two streets [grouped into eight color groups], four railroads, and two utilities], three Chance spaces, three Community Chest spaces, a Luxury Tax space, an Income Tax space, and the four corner squares: GO, [In] Jail/Just Visiting, Free Parking, and Go to Jail.\r\n\r\nA player continues to travel around the board until he or she is bankrupt. Bankruptcy results in elimination from the game. The last player remaining on the board is the winner.\r\n\r\nIf a player lands on a Chance or Community Chest space, they draw the top card from the respective deck and follow its instructions.\r\n\r\nAt the beginning of the game, each player is given a fixed amount of play money; the players then moves around the board according to the throw of a pair of dice. \r\n\r\nAny player who lands on an uncrowned property may buy it, but, if he or she lands on a property owned by another player, rent must be paid to that player, If a player acquires a Business International- that is, If a player owns all the spaces within a color group, he may then build or develop equal houses and hotels on these spaces, generating even more income from opponents who land there must pay that player rent according to the value of the land and any buildings on it. \r\n\r\nBusiness International is a real estate trading game that everyone plays for fun and a chance to be a virtual real estate tycoon.
